 baat sochnewali he, wo isliye ki faqat ek chori se aakhir duniya par itnaa bada khatra kaise paidaa ho gaya? lekin is chori ke peeche kii asli kahani vaaki rongte khadey karanevaali he

 dilli ke purvi jile ne buudhvaar ko pehali 'demokrasi on wheels' ko dilli ke chif elactoral officer ranbir singh ne launch kiya
